423582047660015616  Jan 15 17:26  @gmodproject      #PAGXXII MAKER step 2: generate ab initio gene predictions from Augustus, etc. - can provide own results. Need to “train” the predictors
423582412673515520  Jan 15 17:28  @gmodproject      #PAGXXII MAKER step 3: BLAST; 4: run exonerate to polish the BLAST alignments. Generates “hints” as to where genes are;
423582548506071041  Jan 15 17:28  @gmodproject      #PAGXXII MAKER feeds this back to the gene finding SW

423584555451179009  Jan 15 17:36  @gmodproject      #PAGXXII 1st gen genome projects: Big $$$, big community, big knowledge.
423584937527083008  Jan 15 17:38  @gmodproject      #PAGXXII MAKER annotation evaluation in 1st gen - with lots of training data, ab initio gene predictors can outperform pipelines like MAKER
423585119496978433  Jan 15 17:38  @gmodproject      #PAGXXII BUT next gen. organisms are different - small communities, small $$, not much knowledge.
423585860219441153  Jan 15 17:41  @gmodproject      #PAGXXII MAKER pipeline performs much better on these ‘next gen’ genomes
423586148720459776  Jan 15 17:43  @gmodproject      #PAGXXII Researchers also want to integrate data from mRNA seq (from top hat, cufflinks)
423586287816548353  Jan 15 17:43  @gmodproject      #PAGXXII MAKER can integrate this so that the cufflinks and top hat data informs the final models in MAKER
423586454703337472  Jan 15 17:44  @gmodproject      #PAGXXII Also - MAKER can be used to update/revise legacy genome annotation sets
